## aws 

- [chinchalinchin/mastodon-agent](https://github.com/chinchalinchin/mastodon-agent) - LLM driven bot agent for Mastodon.
- [getsops/sops](https://github.com/getsops/sops) - Simple and flexible tool for managing secrets
